-- ----------------------------- 2022-10-27 add by liuxia--------------begin

-- 建表语句
CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    RESOURCENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    RESOURCEDESC VARCHAR2(180)  NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PARENTID NUMBER NULL,
    ORDERNO NUMBER NULL,
    CONTENT CLOB NULL,
    EFFECTVERSION NUMBER NULL,
    PATH VARCHAR2(360)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE IS '低代码平台资源表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.RESOURCENAME IS '资源名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.RESOURCEDESC IS '资源描述';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型(模块分类、模块、页面、前端脚本、后端脚本)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.PARENTID IS '父ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.ORDERNO IS '排序码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CONTENT IS '内容';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.EFFECTVERSION IS '生效版本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.PATH IS '资源路径';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_RESOURCE PRIMARY KEY (ID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    RESOURCEID NUMBER NULL,
    RESOURCENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    RESOURCEDESC VARCHAR2(180)  NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CONTENT CLOB NULL,
    VERSION NUMBER NULL,
    SUBMITFLAG VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    EFFECTFLAG VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY IS '低代码平台资源历史表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.RESOURCEID IS '资源ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.RESOURCENAME IS '资源名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.RESOURCEDESC IS '资源描述';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型(模块分类、模块、页面、前端脚本、后端脚本)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CONTENT IS '内容';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.VERSION IS '版本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.SUBMITFLAG IS '是否提交';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.EFFECTFLAG IS '是否生效';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY_RESOURCEID ON T_LCDP_RESOURCE_HISTORY (RESOURCEID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP(
    ID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    MODULEPAGEHISTORYID NUMBER NULL,
    MODULEPAGEID NUMBER NULL,
    MODULEPAGEVERSION NUMBER NULL,
    COMPID VARCHAR2(18)  NULL,
    COMPCATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PARENTID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PREVIOUSID NUMBER NULL,
    VISIBLE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    EDITABLE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CONFIG CLOB NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP IS '功能模块页面组件表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.ID IS '前端组件UUID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.MODULEPAGEHISTORYID IS '模块页面历史ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.MODULEPAGEID IS '模块页面ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.MODULEPAGEVERSION IS '模块页面版本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.COMPID IS '组件ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.COMPCATEGORY IS '组件类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.PARENTID IS '父组件ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.PREVIOUSID IS '前一组件id';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.VISIBLE IS '是否可见';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.EDITABLE IS '是否可编辑';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CONFIG IS '组件配置';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP_MODULEPAGEID ON T_LCDP_MODULE_PAGE_COMP (MODULEPAGEID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    RESOURCEID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    LOCKUSERID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK IS '低代码平台资源锁定';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK.RESOURCEID IS '资源ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK.LOCKUSERID IS '锁定人员';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK_RESOURCEID ON T_LCDP_RESOURCE_LOCK (RESOURCEID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    RESOURCEID VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    RESOURCENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    VERSION NUMBER NULL,
    COMMIT VARCHAR2(180)  NULL,
    EFFECTFLAG VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    SUBMITTIME DATE NULL,
    EDITTIME VARCHAR2 NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION IS '低代码平台资源版本表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.RESOURCEID IS '资源ID(对于表是表名tableName,对于资源是资源ID resourceId)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.RESOURCENAME IS '资源名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.VERSION IS '版本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.COMMIT IS '提交日志';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.EFFECTFLAG IS '是否生效';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.SUBMITTIME IS '提交时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.EDITTIME IS '开始编辑时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION_RESOURCEID ON T_LCDP_RESOURCE_VERSION (RESOURCEID);

-- 建表语句
CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    BPCODE VARCHAR2(30)  NULL,
    BPNAME VARCHAR2(120)  NULL,
    BPDESC VARCHAR2(300)  NULL,
    RESOURCEID NUMBER NULL,
    RESOURCENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    TABLENAME VARCHAR2(150)  NULL,
    ACTIVATEDFLAG VARCHAR2(1)  NULL,
    ACTIVATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    ACTIVATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    ACTIVATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    VERSION NUMBER NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS IS '工作流';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.ID IS '主键ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.BPCODE IS '工作流编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.BPNAME IS '工作流名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.BPDESC IS '工作流描述';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.RESOURCEID IS '绑定页面ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.RESOURCENAME IS '绑定页面名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.TABLENAME IS '绑定表名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.ACTIVATEDFLAG IS '启用标志';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.ACTIVATEDBYID IS '启用/停用人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.ACTIVATEDBYNAME IS '启用/停用人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.ACTIVATEDTIME IS '启用/停用时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.VERSION IS '版本号';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS PRIMARY KEY (ID);

COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS_NODE.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS_NODE.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS_NODE.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS_NODE.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

-- 表管理
CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    TABLENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NOT NULL,
    TABLEDESC VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    VERSION NUMBER NULL,
    SQL CLOB NULL,
    SUBMITFLAG VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE IS '低代码平台表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.TABLENAME IS '表名';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.TABLEDESC IS '表注释';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.VERSION IS '版本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.SQL IS 'SQL';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE.SUBMITFLAG IS '是否提交';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_TABLE PRIMARY KEY (ID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    TABLEID NUMBER NULL,
    FIELDNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    FIELDCOMMENT VARCHAR2(120)  NULL,
    FIELDTYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    FIELDLENGTH VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    ALLOWNULL VARCHAR2(1)  NULL,
    DEFAULTVALUE VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    FIELDOPERATIONTYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
	CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD IS '低代码平台表字段';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.TABLEID IS '表ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.FIELDNAME IS '字段名';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.FIELDCOMMENT IS '字段注释';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.FIELDTYPE IS '字段类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.FIELDLENGTH IS '字段长度';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.ALLOWNULL IS '是否可为空';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.DEFAULTVALUE IS '默认值';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.FIELDOPERATIONTYPE IS '字段操作类型(add、delete、update)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD_TABLEID ON T_LCDP_TABLE_FIELD (TABLEID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    TABLEID NUMBER NULL,
    INDEXNAME VARCHAR2(120)  NULL,
    INDEXTYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    INDEXFIELD VARCHAR2(120)  NULL,
    INDEXOPERATIONTYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
	CREATEDBYID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    CREATEDTIME DATE  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CREATEDBYORGNAME VARCHAR2(270)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX IS '低代码平台表索引';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.TABLEID IS '表ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.INDEXNAME IS '索引名';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.INDEXTYPE IS '索引类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.INDEXFIELD IS '索引字段';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.INDEXOPERATIONTYPE IS '索引操作类型(add、delete、update)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.CREATEDBYID IS '制单人编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.CREATEDBYNAME IS '制单人名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.CREATEDTIME IS '制单时间';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.CREATEDBYORGID IS '制单人单位编码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX.CREATEDBYORGNAME IS '制单人单位名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX_TABLEID ON T_LCDP_TABLE_INDEX (TABLEID);

-- 表字段默认值字段为LONG类型 转为 VARCHAR2
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION LONG_TO_CHAR(uTABLE IN VARCHAR2,uID IN NUMBER)
RETURN VARCHAR2
AS
  uVal VARCHAR2(4000);
BEGIN
  SELECT DATA_DEFAULT INTO uVal FROM USER_TAB_COLS WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(uTABLE) AND COLUMN_ID = uID;
  RETURN uVal;
END LONG_TO_CHAR;

-- 文件操作系统脚本
INSERT INTO T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD (ID,RESOURCEID,PATH) VALUES (SEQ_CORE.NEXTVAL,1,'lcdp.file.server.FileScript.delete');
INSERT INTO T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD (ID,RESOURCEID,PATH) VALUES (SEQ_CORE.NEXTVAL,1,'lcdp.file.server.FileScript.upload');
INSERT INTO T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD (ID,RESOURCEID,PATH) VALUES (SEQ_CORE.NEXTVAL,1,'lcdp.file.server.FileScript.selectPagination');
INSERT INTO T_LCDP_RESOURCE (ID,RESOURCENAME,RESOURCEDESC,RESOURCECATEGORY,PARENTID,ORDERNO,CONTENT,EFFECTVERSION,"PATH",CREATEDBYID,CREATEDBYNAME,CREATEDTIME,CREATEDBYORGID,CREATEDBYORGNAME) VALUES (1,'FileScript','文件操作系统脚本','java',0,1,TO_CLOB('import com.sunwayworld.framework.context.ApplicationContextHelper;
import com.sunwayworld.framework.data.page.Page;
import com.sunwayworld.framework.restful.data.RestJsonWrapperBean;
import com.sunwayworld.module.item.file.bean.CoreFileBean;
import com.sunwayworld.module.item.file.service.CoreFileService;
import org.springframework.web.multipart.MultipartFile;
import com.sunwayworld.cloud.module.lcdp.base.LcdpResultDTO;
import com.sunwayworld.cloud.module.lcdp.support.constant.LcdpConstant;


public class FileScript{


    /**
     * 查询附件数据
     *
     * @param wrapper
     */
    public Page<CoreFileBean> selectPagination(RestJsonWrapperBean wrapper) {

        Page<CoreFileBean> filePage = ApplicationContextHelper.getBean(CoreFileService.class).selectSearchablePagination(wrapper);

        return filePage;
    }

    /**
     * 上传附件
     */
    public Long upload(CoreFileBean coreFile, MultipartFile file) {

        Long fileId = ApplicationContextHelper.getBean(CoreFileService.class).upload(coreFile, file);

        return fileId;
    }

    /**
     * 删除附件
     */
    public LcdpResultDTO delete(RestJsonWrapperBean wrapper) {
        ApplicationContextHelper.getBean(CoreFileService.class).delete(wrapper);
        return new LcdpResultDTO(LcdpConstant.RESULT_CODE_SUCCESS, LcdpConstant.RESULT_MESSAGE_SUCCESS);
    }
}'),1,'lcdp.file.server.FileScript',null,null,null,null,null);


COMMIT;

-- 建表语句
CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    MODULETMPLNAME VARCHAR2(120)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL IS '模块模板';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL.MODULETMPLNAME IS '模板名称';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL PRIMARY KEY (ID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    MODULETMPLCONFIGID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CONTENT CLOB NULL,
    PAGETYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE IS '模块模板资源';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE.MODULETMPLCONFIGID IS '模块模板配置ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型页面、前端脚本、后端脚本';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE.CONTENT IS '内容';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE.PAGETYPE IS '页面类型';

ALTER TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE ADD CONSTRAINT PK_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE PRIMARY KEY (ID);
CREATE INDEX IDX_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE_MODULETMPLCONFIGID ON T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_RESOURCE (MODULETMPLCONFIGID);

CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_PAGE_COMP(
    ID VARCHAR2(36)  NOT NULL,
    MODULETMPLPAGEID NUMBER NULL,
    COMPID VARCHAR2(18)  NULL,
    TYPE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PARENTID VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PREVIOUSID NUMBER NULL,
    VISIBLE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    EDITABLE VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    CONFIG VARCHAR2(4000)  NULL,
    CONFIGEXTEND VARCHAR2(4000)  NULL,
    COMPTAG VARCHAR2(36)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_PAGE_COMP IS '模块模板页面组件表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_MODULE_TMPL_PAGE_COMP.ID IS '主键';

 );

alter table T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD add METHODNAME VARCHAR2(60);
comment on column T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD.METHODNAME is '方法名称';
alter table T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD add METHODPATH VARCHAR2(120);
comment on column T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD.METHODPATH is '方法路径';
alter table T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD add SERVERSCRIPTID NUMBER;
comment on column T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD.SERVERSCRIPTID is '服务端脚本ID';

UPDATE T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD SET METHODPATH = "PATH"  ;

UPDATE T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD SET SERVERSCRIPTID = RESOURCEID ;

alter table T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD drop column path;
alter table T_LCDP_SERVER_SCRIPT_METHOD drop column resourceId;

alter table T_CORE_MENU add MENUPARAM VARCHAR2(120);
comment on column T_CORE_MENU.MENUPARAM is '菜单参数';


CALL INSERTI18N('T_CORE_MENU.MENUPARAM', '菜单参数', '菜单参数', 'zh-CN', '菜单参数');
CALL UPDATEI18N('T_LCDP_BIZ_PROCESS_NODE_MENU.FILTERSCRIPT', 'zh-CN', '菜单参数');

CALL INSERTI18N('LCDP.MODULE.RESOUCES.TIP.JS_EDITING', '已检出的JS脚本', '已检出的JS脚本', 'zh-CN', '已检出的JS脚本');
CALL INSERTI18N('LCDP.MODULE.RESOUCES.TIP.JAVA_EDITING', '已检出的JAVA脚本', '已检出的JAVA脚本', 'zh-CN', '已检出的JAVA脚本');
CALL INSERTI18N('LCDP.MODULE.RESOUCES.TIP.TABLE_EDITING', '已检出的表', '已检出的表', 'zh-CN', '已检出的表');

-- ----------------------------- 2022-12-29 add by liuxia------------begin
CREATE TABLE T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE(
    ID NUMBER NOT NULL,
    MODULETMPLID NUMBER NULL,
    RESOURCENAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL,
    RESOURCEDESC VARCHAR2(180)  NULL,
    RESOURCECATEGORY VARCHAR2(36)  NULL,
    PARENTID NUMBER NULL,
    ORDERNO NUMBER NULL,
    CONTENT CLOB NULL,
    EFFECTVERSION NUMBER NULL,
    PATH VARCHAR2(360)  NULL,
    CLASSNAME VARCHAR2(60)  NULL
 );
COMMENT ON TABLE T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE IS '自定义模板资源表';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.ID IS '主键';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.MODULETMPLID IS '模块模板ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.RESOURCENAME IS '资源名称';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.RESOURCEDESC IS '资源描述';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.RESOURCECATEGORY IS '资源类型';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.PARENTID IS '父ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.ORDERNO IS '排序码';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.CONTENT IS '内容';
COMMENT ON COLUMN T_LCDP_CUSTOM_TMPL_RESOURCE.EFFECTVERSION IS '生效版本';
